name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:28 Reviews
rating:4.1
posted:Posted June 2, 2024
msg:This is my third time in Chongli. After comparing the two hotels, I chose Yuansu over Crowne Plaza. The main reason is that it is owned by Westin. I like Westin very much, so I want to experience it. After I came here, I felt that every aspect of the hotel reflects the simple style, and the environmental protection concept is reflected to the extreme, but it still has a sense of design. The room also has an open kitchen, which gives it a warm feeling of home.
But there are three points that are not good:
1) The night light could not be turned off on the first night, which made it difficult for the child to fall asleep because the light in the room was on;
2) The curtains were not designed to be floor-length, which caused the lights on the town streets outside the window to shine in all the time, affecting sleep.
3) The water in the shower room in the bathroom is not well drained. A little foam will accumulate water, which greatly affects the bathing experience.
4) The breakfast is a bit simple, and I found that the dishes were often not replenished immediately for two days, and the guests often had to take the initiative to make requests.
Let's talk about the good aspects:
1) The hotel is located in Taiwu Town, which is very convenient, and there are rich catering and entertainment facilities around.
2) There are charging piles in the basement.
3) There is a swimming pool, but we didn't have time to experience it due to time constraints.
4) High cost performance. Not only did the price not increase on Children's Day, but we also got cable car tickets and hot spring tickets, as well as some other items. However, since the other benefits need to be booked one day in advance, we didn't experience them, which is a bit tasteless.
Overall, it's not bad.

msg:Service: First of all, thank you to Nancy, the front desk of the hotel, for proactively answering all questions.

Facilities: Among the several small towns in the Chongli area, whether it is Taiwu Town or the nearby Fulong Four Seasons Town and Cuiyun Mountain Resort, they are mainly family-friendly. Most of them are large bed + small bed room type. For guests like me who are traveling with just two adults and need to book a twin room, this Westin Element Hotel has a twin room with two 1.5M wide beds, which is so rare! Good review!

Its location is definitely the best in Taiwu Town. There is a small square behind it. Go left and you will find the main street. It takes a few minutes to walk to the cable car station.

The facilities in the guest rooms exceeded expectations, including induction cookers, upper and lower double-door large-capacity refrigerators, and integrated barbecue and microwave built-in stoves. The kitchen countertops are particularly wide. The only drawback is that there is not much difference in the depth of the wall cabinets and the bottom countertops. As a tall person like me, I might not pay attention if I don't pay attention. Headbanging...

The mattress is really comfortable, comparable to the comfort of a Japanese hotel. Sofas and office chairs are also ergonomically designed.

There is also a Philips humidifier in the room, a must-have when drying out in winter! People like me who are particularly afraid of dry noses don‚Äôt have to worry about nosebleeds even in winter!

Two major selling points of the hotel: it‚Äôs pet-friendly and can bring dogs! However, I didn‚Äôt see anyone bringing large dogs. I wonder if Rottweilers and pit bulls can come. There are wall-mounted charging piles in the underground garage, including ordinary DC fast charging and NIO's super charging.

There are three shortcomings. The first is that there is no washlet on the toilet, and you have to go to the rain area to flush your butt after using the toilet... The second is that the room is too hot. After I checked in, I saw that the room temperature was as high as 27¬∞C, and there was no air conditioning in mid-September. The air conditioner turned on, so I had to sleep with the balcony door open. Fortunately, the outdoor temperature dropped to 3¬∞C before sunrise to cool down the room. The third thing is that my super-sensitive sense of smell smelled the aftertaste of dog urine in a corner of the desk. Are you sure that every time a guest who brings a dog is carefully inspected and thoroughly cleaned and deodorized after leaving?

msg:advantage:
1. It‚Äôs pet-friendly and you can bring your dog in. Just add a cleaning fee of 150 per night, which is very reasonable;
2. The location is good. There is a ski equipment hall just over 100 meters away. It is very convenient to go to the ski resort;
3. Breakfast is okay, the meat dumplings are delicious;
4. The room is fully equipped with kitchen facilities, a small bar, etc., and the overall style is Nordic.
Shortcomings or areas for improvement:
1. You can only check in at 3 pm, but the ski resort in Taiwu closes at 5 pm, so the time on the check-in day is very tight. I had to check out at 12 o'clock the next day, and the time I could ski in the morning was also very short. Halfway through the skiing, I had to run back to pack my things and check out at around 11:20. It felt like I couldn't ski for a few hours during the entire stay;
2. The room facilities are a bit old, with a feeling of wear and tear that has been used for all seasons for 4 or 5 years (maybe this is the Nordic style?), which feels quite different from the room price of 1,300+;
3. The bed in room 603 squeaks when turned over;
4. There is no hot spring in the hotel. The hot spring discount provided by the sliding package is to go to Xueluju, which is relatively far away. It is too cold outside and I am too lazy to go, which makes the night a little boring.
All in all, it is a good choice for bringing pets, but it is recommended to further optimize check-in and check-out times, and consider enriching health and wellness facilities.

msg:The location of the hotel is very good. It takes only five minutes to go to the center of the town. The facilities are complete and the service is very good. The breakfast is good, but there are many people and sometimes there are no seats, but the service staff can find seats. There are parking spaces on the ground and underground parking, and the open-air barbecue at night is also ok.
